            reactions induced via Bremsstrahlung from the         2308300100024

            uranium target.                                       2308300100026

DETECTOR   (IOCH) The alpha-particles were detected using a       2308300100036 
            Frisch-gridded ionization chamber filled with ultra   2308300100037 
            pure C-H4 as detector gas.                            2308300100038 
           (BF3) BF3 proportional counters were located at        2308300100039 
            different places above the neutron source. Their      2308300100040 
            output is used to normalize spectra to the same total 2308300100041 
            neutron flux.                                         2308300100042
